    EventClass_IsStar : Boolean value: 1 = true, 0 = false: Is it a star

    EventClass_BodyDesignationOrName : String value: EDD logical name or journal name

    EventClass_BodyID : Integer value: Internal Frontier ID, is empty for older scans
    EventClass_StarSystem : String value: Name of star
    EventClass_SystemAddress : Integer value: Internal Frontier ID, is empty for older scans

    EventClass_DistanceFromArrivalm : Floating point value: In meters
    EventClass_DistanceFromArrivalText : String value: Astronomic Unit (AU) and Ls
